## **KEY DESIGN CHANGES FROM PREVIOUS VERSION:**

### **Transaction Display**
- âœ… **Table-based** instead of accordion/cards for scalability
- âœ… **Pagination** (50 transactions per page) for large CTRs (500-1000+)
- âœ… **Sortable columns**: Date, Amount, Type, Originator, Beneficiary
- âœ… **Filterable** by type, amount range, subject, date range
- âœ… **Search** functionality across transaction fields
- âœ… **Side panel (Sheet)** for detailed transaction view (opens on row click)
- âœ… **Alert indicators** (ðŸš¨) in table rows for quick visual scanning

### **Performance Optimizations**
- Virtual scrolling or pagination prevents rendering 1000+ rows at once
- Lazy loading of transaction details in side panel
- Efficient filtering/sorting on server-side or optimized client-side

### **User Experience**
- Quick scanning of all transactions without expanding cards
- Easy comparison of multiple transactions side-by-side
- Bulk selection capability for batch operations
- Clear visual hierarchy: overview â†’ table â†’ detail panel
